Needed a car wash to take the bug juice off and to vacuum the snack crumbs from the seats after a full day of highway driving.  Chose the wash that included cleaning the mats.  The good: They took extra time to get the bugs off, cleaned the wheels really well, fast workers, car was cleaner than what I could do myself. < review>
Had to replace all 4 tires on my fiat, so naturally I called around to price shop. I called almost every shop in Ukiah, and priced out buying tires online and having them installed. FYI most places charge 40$ a tire to install.
Big O had the second best price in town, off by about 30$. However they could get the tires in next day, and could install them. Other places were booked into next week.
Cody there has taken care of my truck for years, and they‚Äôve never done me wrong. They found when putting my tires on that I needed new brakes, and the pads weren‚Äôt wearing evenly. They explained what was going on in detail, and gave me a reasonable quote. I appreciated that they took the time to do the inspection, and make sure my car is working correctly. I rely on mechanics to let me know what they see, and the multi point inspections are vital. Not everywhere does that, although they state they do.
I trust Big O with my vehicles. A definite stop if your looking for good service, at a fair price, and need tires, visit these guys.<//review>

< review>
Buying tires while on vacation is never the shopping that you want to do. There were two tire stores in Mendocino, one was closed on Saturday, the other wasn't a place that we could come back to for warrantee repairs. So we drove the 90 minutes on a donut all the way into Ukiah.

This is a great lounge. I have been here on a few dates and have always felt welcomed. The ambiance is casually romantic and fun. < text>
4 stars because it's fine for California pizza.  But I must say...if you're familiar with real NY-style pizza, and expecting anything close to that based on the other reviews...you're gonna have a bad time.

1)  They don't sell slices, they only sell personal pizzas.  You can't even find personal pizzas in New York...wanna know why?   A personal pizza is about 40% crust.  It just ruins the ratio.  Personal pizzas are for children who don't know any better.
2)  The crust is way too thin and crunchy.  New York style pizza crust is thin, but has some substance, and is soft enough to bend!  It's not supposed to be like eating a pizza-flavored cracker.
3)  The sauce is sweet and bland.  It lacks any hint of basil or herbs that good NY pizza has.  Also...they put the sauce on top of the cheese.  I don't even know what to say about that.

On the flip side, the cheese is very good though.  They make it fresh, and it shows.  They just need to fix everything else, and maybe it will be good "NY style" pizza.  Until then, for east-coasters at least, it's just another gimmicky and ultimately disappointing California pizza place.<//text>
